            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Tom Seaver
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <script>
           BR.articleData.media_slots[25] = {
            script: false,
            markup: "&lt;iframe id=\"3GB_kkbFVhk\" class=\"video_embed\" title=\"YouTube video player\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/3GB_kkbFVhk?wmode=transparent&amp;autoplay=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;",
            type: "youtube"
        };
          </script>
          <div class="article_media-slot article_media-slot--video article_media-slot--top article_media-slot--youtube" data-is-ooyala="false">
           <ul class="share-buttons share-buttons--video share-buttons--youtube cf border-box ">
            <li class="share-button button button--facebook " data-position="vid" data-source="facebook" data-url="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history">
             <a href="#" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--facebook ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Share
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--twitter " data-position="vid" data-source="twitter">
             <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?original_referer=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;text=30+Quirkiest+Pitching+Deliveries+in+MLB+History&amp;tw_p=tweetbutton&amp;via=bleacherreport&amp;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history%3Futm_source%3Dtwitter.com%26utm_medium%3Dshare%26utm_campaign%3Dweb-des-art-vid-18" target="_blank" title="Share on Twitter">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--twitter ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Tweet
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--email " data-position="vid" data-source="email">
             <a href="mailto:?title=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History&amp;body=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history" title="Email">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--email ">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Elected to the Hall of Fame with the highest percentage of votes anyone has ever received98.84 percent311 game-winner Tom Seaver had a delivery that was remarkable in both its effectiveness and mechanics.
           </p>
           <p>
            Seaver utilized his legs as well as any pitcher ever has.
           </p>
           <p>
            During his windup, as he would bring his right leg down, he would stretch it as far as he could toward home plate, forcing his right leg to drop to the ground, oftentimes resulting in his knee resting on the pitcher's mound.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-26 cf display-none " data-page="26">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
              Prev
             </a>
             <div class="paginators_counter">
              26
              <span class="br-light-grey">
               of
              </span>
              <span class="paginators_page-count">
               32
              </span>
             </div>
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--next" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Next Page">
              Next
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Dean Chance
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:400px">
            <img alt="Dean Chance" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/167/776/chance_crop_north.jpg?w=400&amp;h=313&amp;q=75" height="313" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="400"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            A two-time All-Star and winner of the American League Cy Young award in 1964 with the Angels, batters hated coming to the plate against Dean Chance.
           </p>
           <p>
            It wasn't necessarily because of Chance's stuff, of which his slider was his best pitch.
           </p>
           <p>
            As soon as he would get the sign from the catcher and started his windup, he would twist around so that his back was facing home plateand the batter.
           </p>
           <p>
            Chance would then spin around and fire the ball toward the plate, often never getting more than a faint glimpse of where the catcher was set up.
           </p>
           <p>
            Hitters not only had no idea what pitch was coming, they had no idea where the pitch was headed, since whether Chance actually looked at home plate before throwing the ball was unclear.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-27 cf is-media display-none " data-page="27">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
              Prev
             </a>
             <div class="paginators_counter">

              <span class="br-light-grey">
               of
              </span>
              <span class="paginators_page-count">

              </span>
             </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Walter Johnson
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <script>
           BR.articleData.media_slots[27] = {
            script: false,
            markup: "&lt;iframe id=\"Gc8MbjXMfzs\" class=\"video_embed\" title=\"YouTube video player\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/Gc8MbjXMfzs?wmode=transparent&amp;autoplay=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;",
            type: "youtube"
        };
          </script>
          <div class="article_media-slot article_media-slot--video article_media-slot--top article_media-slot--youtube" data-is-ooyala="false">
           <ul class="share-buttons share-buttons--video share-buttons--youtube cf border-box ">
            <li class="share-button button button--facebook " data-position="vid" data-source="facebook" data-url="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history">
             <a href="#" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--facebook ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Share
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--twitter " data-position="vid" data-source="twitter">
             <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?original_referer=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;text=30+Quirkiest+Pitching+Deliveries+in+MLB+History&amp;tw_p=tweetbutton&amp;via=bleacherreport&amp;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history%3Futm_source%3Dtwitter.com%26utm_medium%3Dshare%26utm_campaign%3Dweb-des-art-vid-18" target="_blank" title="Share on Twitter">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--twitter ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Tweet
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--email " data-position="vid" data-source="email">
             <a href="mailto:?title=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History&amp;body=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history" title="Email">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--email ">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Arguably the best pitcher in the history of the game, Walter "Big Train" Johnson won 417 games, and his name is near or at the top of multiple pitching records.
           </p>
           <p>
            His delivery wasn't so much quirky as it was deceptive.
           </p>
           <p>
            Johnson generated his power and momentum from utilizing his entire body and having near perfect mechanics. His arm, which he brought forward a bit lower than a sidearm pitcher would, was doing less work, thus not having nearly as much strain put on it.
           </p>
           <p>
            Essentially, Johnson looked like he wasn't throwing the ball hardand that he was barely using his arm.
           </p>
           <p>
            Columnist Ring Lardner commented on that very thing:
            <font color="#000000" size="-1">
             "He's got a gun concealed about his person.
             <a href="http://www.baseball-almanac.com/quotes/quojhns.shtml">
              They can't tell me
             </a>
             he throws them balls with his arm."
            </font>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            One of the great feel-good stories in sports history, Jim Abbott, who was born without a right hand, not only pitched in the major leagues, but he threw a no-hitter as well.
           </p>
           <p>
            Never thinking of himself as disabled or handicapped, Abbott figured out how to play his position.
           </p>
           <p>
            During his delivery, he would balance his glove on his right arm, and as soon as the ball left his hand, he'd quickly put the glove on his left hand so he was prepared to field.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-29 cf is-media display-none " data-page="29">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

              </span>

             </a>

             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Carl Hubbell
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <script>
           BR.articleData.media_slots[29] = {
            script: false,
            markup: "&lt;iframe id=\"OEO5EmgjeVc\" class=\"video_embed\" title=\"YouTube video player\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/OEO5EmgjeVc?wmode=transparent&amp;autoplay=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;",
            type: "youtube"
        };
          </script>
          <div class="article_media-slot article_media-slot--video article_media-slot--top article_media-slot--youtube" data-is-ooyala="false">
           <ul class="share-buttons share-buttons--video share-buttons--youtube cf border-box ">
            <li class="share-button button button--facebook " data-position="vid" data-source="facebook" data-url="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history">
             <a href="#" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--facebook ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Share
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--twitter " data-position="vid" data-source="twitter">
             <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?original_referer=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;text=30+Quirkiest+Pitching+Deliveries+in+MLB+History&amp;tw_p=tweetbutton&amp;via=bleacherreport&amp;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history%3Futm_source%3Dtwitter.com%26utm_medium%3Dshare%26utm_campaign%3Dweb-des-art-vid-18" target="_blank" title="Share on Twitter">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--twitter ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Tweet
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--email " data-position="vid" data-source="email">
             <a href="mailto:?title=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History&amp;body=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history" title="Email">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--email ">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            An eight-time All-Star, two-time National League MVP and a member of the Hall of Fame, Carl Hubbell spent his entire 16-year career with the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1147248-new-york-giants-nfl-draft-updates-latest-news-trade-rumors-storylines%09">
             New York Giants
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            In the 1934 All-Star Game, Hubbell struck out five Hall of Famers in a row: Babe Ruth, Lou Gehrig, Nellie Fox, Al Simmons and Joe Cronin, relying on his favorite pitch, the screwball.
           </p>
           <p>
            Hubbell's delivery was so violent that by the time he retired in 1943 at the age of 40, his left arm had been permanently disfigured from the abuse he put it through.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-30 cf is-media display-none " data-page="30">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
              Prev
             </a>
             <div class="paginators_counter">
              30
              <span class="br-light-grey">
               of
              </span>
              <span class="paginators_page-count">
               32
              </span>
             </div>
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--next" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Next Page">
              Next
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Mordecai "Three Finger" Brown
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <script>
           BR.articleData.media_slots[30] = {
            script: false,
            markup: "&lt;iframe id=\"FzkyW7WcybU\" class=\"video_embed\" title=\"YouTube video player\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/FzkyW7WcybU?wmode=transparent&amp;autoplay=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;",
            type: "youtube"
        };
          </script>
          <div class="article_media-slot article_media-slot--video article_media-slot--top article_media-slot--youtube" data-is-ooyala="false">
           <ul class="share-buttons share-buttons--video share-buttons--youtube cf border-box ">
            <li class="share-button button button--facebook " data-position="vid" data-source="facebook" data-url="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history">
             <a href="#" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--facebook ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Share
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--twitter " data-position="vid" data-source="twitter">
             <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?original_referer=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;text=30+Quirkiest+Pitching+Deliveries+in+MLB+History&amp;tw_p=tweetbutton&amp;via=bleacherreport&amp;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history%3Futm_source%3Dtwitter.com%26utm_medium%3Dshare%26utm_campaign%3Dweb-des-art-vid-18" target="_blank" title="Share on Twitter">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--twitter ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Tweet
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--email " data-position="vid" data-source="email">
             <a href="mailto:?title=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History&amp;body=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history" title="Email">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--email ">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Inducted into the Hall of Fame in 1949, Mordecai Brown won two World Series championships with the Chicago Cubs and kept hitters off balance for more than a decade.
           </p>
           <p>
            From 1906 through 1911, Brown won no fewer than 20 games in a season, going a combined 148-55 with a 1.63 ERA and a 0.97 WHIP.
           </p>
           <p>
            As we can see from the video, he had a very unique delivery (pay attention to his right arm).
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-31 cf is-media display-none " data-page="31">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">

              <span class="br-light-grey">

              <span class="paginators_page-count">

              </span>

              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Mark "The Bird" Fidrych
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <script>
           BR.articleData.media_slots[31] = {
            script: false,
            markup: "&lt;iframe id=\"sMSDo3BX5Ds\" class=\"video_embed\" title=\"YouTube video player\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/sMSDo3BX5Ds?wmode=transparent&amp;autoplay=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;",
            type: "youtube"
        };
          </script>
          <div class="article_media-slot article_media-slot--video article_media-slot--top article_media-slot--youtube" data-is-ooyala="false">
           <ul class="share-buttons share-buttons--video share-buttons--youtube cf border-box ">
            <li class="share-button button button--facebook " data-position="vid" data-source="facebook" data-url="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history">
             <a href="#" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--facebook ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Share
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--twitter " data-position="vid" data-source="twitter">
             <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?original_referer=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;text=30+Quirkiest+Pitching+Deliveries+in+MLB+History&amp;tw_p=tweetbutton&amp;via=bleacherreport&amp;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history%3Futm_source%3Dtwitter.com%26utm_medium%3Dshare%26utm_campaign%3Dweb-des-art-vid-18" target="_blank" title="Share on Twitter">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--twitter ">
              </span>
              <span class="share-text">
               Tweet
              </span>
              <span class="share-count">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-button button button--email " data-position="vid" data-source="email">
             <a href="mailto:?title=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History&amp;body=30%20Quirkiest%20Pitching%20Deliveries%20in%20MLB%20History%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fbleacherreport.com%2Farticles%2F1159429-mlb-the-30-quirkiest-pitching-deliveries-in-baseball-history" title="Email">
              <span class="br-sprite br-sprite--email ">
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Maybe he doesn't belong on this list, as his antics were on display in between pitches, but you can't compile a list involving quirky pitchers and not mention Mark Fidrych.
           </p>
           <p>
            His career lasted only five years due to injury, but he will forever be remembered as one of the most entertaining players the game has ever seen.
           </p>
           <p>
            On the mound, Fidrych would talk to himself. He'd talk to the ball. Sometimes, he'd stand on the mound and hold the ball as if he were about to throw a dart at a dartboard.
           </p>
           <p>
            Other times, he'd crouch down on the mound and begin to smooth out the cleat marks left by others. If a ball had been hit too many times, he'd refuse to pitch until it was removed from the game.
           </p>
           <p>
            Like I said, you can't possibly write about quirky baseball players and not include Mark Fidrych.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

    // Load the SDK asynchronously
    (function(){
        // If we've already installed the SDK, we're done
        if (document.getElementById('facebook-jssdk')) {return;}

        // Get the first script element, which we'll use to find the parent node
        var firstScriptElement = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];

        // Create a new script element and set its id
        var facebookJS = document.createElement('script');
        facebookJS.id = 'facebook-jssdk';
